As a dedication to privacy, info? fields should be denoted as optional non-required fields. However for the sake of Quizzer's attempt to develop a good algorithm, this data may be extremely useful factors in the output of future model development. For this reason we will still ask to collect the information while leaving it as a optional ^pA9WviDd

BACK ^XyFb5ToK

Some Question from the Quizzer database will be
 displayed here in the middle of the screen ^Bmq5Lk4j

The whole center of the screen is a button. When
 the "button" is pressed the answer to the displayed
question will be displayed instead. The answer butto-
ns will also become active. The user will not able to
submit a response until they "flip" over to see the 
answer.
A hidden timer will also begin at 0 when a question 
gets displayed, when the center button is clicked
the timer is stopped and the response time is
recorded locally.

Once a submission below is entered, the response
time and the answer submission is recorded ^IXlO9GZZ

Pre-Process has pre-filtered out ineligible results
reducing the pool of questions down to check 
eligibility to just those within 24hrs ^cR8l2cy9

Request Item
(delete from cache) ^Cw4csmr3

General Pattern:
1. A worker requests an item from a cache (this will remove it from that cache)
2. The worker decides what to do with the record
3. based on decision places that userRecord into a different Cache
4. In most cases the userRecord would get placed back into unProcessed Cache for redistribution
5. This pattern ensures a userRecord only ever exists in a single cache ^9oRjq2pY

Place requested record into eligible Questions list if eligible
ELSE ^iyBkFAf3

If Question not eligible when check is made place back into unprocessed cache ^Ofy5cm88

Request Copy of Eligible Questions ^V7DCSks7

(Run the eligible questions through a selection 
algorithm) ^y6XGNlpx

Update in DB ^CZQJ7ATU

await update of userRecord Table ^SLMYc9d3

After validation get user Records ^SC4DIiod

Spin up order 
(Each worker gets to process the initial loop 
before calling the next worker to spin up)

1. Pre-Process Worker spins up first
2. Eligibility Worker spins up 2nd (gets the initial eligible questions cache filled)
3. Circulation Worker spins up 3rd (needs the eligible questions to decide)
4. Presentation Worker last (needs the eligible questions as well to decide) ^exqFjZTo

Inactive 
Module Worker ^37ejsoIt

Signal that specific module has been activated ^b0xlUpT5

request individual record by module name ^QIwLGX1c

Send record back to unprocessedCache ^MNdTjaXY

When it receives a signal that a specific module has
been deactivated, it will iterate over the records in
the inactive cache under that module name and send
them back to the unprocessed cache. This is done
one by one, not a rapid dumping of records. This 
gives the system time to process what's going on. ^1oeEWgAg

toggleModuleActivation ^3zsbS9xN

Tell the switch board that a module has been toggled on or off ^3lXYagXX
